add_namespace = ottoman

country_event = { #ottoman revolt
	id = ottoman.0
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		random_controlled_state = {
			limit = { resistance > 74.9 }
			controller = { set_temp_variable = { global.occupier_country = THIS } }
			set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_state = THIS }
			if = {
				limit = { has_resistance = yes }
				set_resistance = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
					is_core_of = ALB
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_brutal_surpression_of_albania }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = TUR_amnesty_for_albanian_rebels
						TUR_regime_is_nationalist = yes
					}
					add_ideas = TUR_brutal_surpression
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_amnesty_for_albanian_rebels } }
					add_ideas = TUR_brutal_surpression
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_amnesty_for_albanian_rebels }
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = TUR_brutal_surpression_of_albania
						TUR_regime_is_nationalist = yes
					}
					add_ideas = TUR_policy_of_reapproachment
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = TUR_brutal_surpression_of_albania } }
					add_ideas = TUR_policy_of_reapproachment
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						original_tag = ALB
						has_capitulated = yes
						has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country
					}
				}
				random_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = ALB
					limit = {
						has_capitulated = yes
						has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country
					}
					transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
					set_capital = { state = var:global.occupied_state remember_old_capital = no }
					if = {
						limit = { capital_scope = { ALB_is_kosovar_state = yes } }
						set_cosmetic_tag = ALB_boletini_flag
						every_other_country = {
							limit = { any_character = { ALB_is_kosovar_character = yes } }
							every_character = {
								limit = { ALB_is_kosovar_character = yes }
								set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_country_flag = ALB_refused_the_return_of_abdulhamid }
							promote_character = { character = ALB_idriz_seferi ideology = warlordism }
							promote_character = { character = ALB_idriz_seferi ideology = stratocracy }
						}
						else = {
							promote_character = { character = ALB_isa_boletini ideology = warlordism }
							promote_character = { character = ALB_isa_boletini ideology = stratocracy }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { capital_scope = { ALB_is_northern_state = yes } }
						set_cosmetic_tag = ALB_kimza_flag
						every_other_country = {
							limit = { any_character = { ALB_is_northern_character = yes } }
							every_character = {
								limit = { ALB_is_northern_character = yes }
								set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
						promote_character = { character = ALB_ded_gjo_luli ideology = warlordism }
						promote_character = { character = ALB_ded_gjo_luli ideology = stratocracy }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { capital_scope = { ALB_is_central_state = yes } }
						set_cosmetic_tag = ALB_toptani_flag
						every_other_country = {
							limit = { any_character = { ALB_is_central_character = yes } }
							every_character = {
								limit = { ALB_is_central_character = yes }
								set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
						promote_character = { character = ALB_esad_toptani ideology = warlordism }
						promote_character = { character = ALB_esad_toptani ideology = stratocracy }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { capital_scope = { ALB_is_southern_state = yes } }
						set_cosmetic_tag = ALB_vlora_flag
						every_other_country = {
							limit = { any_character = { ALB_is_southern_character = yes } }
							every_character = {
								limit = { ALB_is_southern_character = yes }
								set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
						promote_character = { character = ALB_cerciz_topulli ideology = warlordism }
						promote_character = { character = ALB_cerciz_topulli ideology = stratocracy }
					}
					set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
					if = {
						limit = { is_government_in_exile = yes }
						every_owned_state = {
							limit = {
								NOT = {
									is_controlled_by = THIS
									state = var:global.occupied_state
								}
							}
							set_state_controller_to = PREV
							transfer_state_to = var:global.occupier_country
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ALB
					ALB = {
						has_capitulated = no
						has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_idea = ALB_decentralized_independence_movement }
							AND = {
								has_idea = ALB_decentralized_independence_movement
								OR = {
									AND = {
										capital_scope = { ALB_is_kosovar_state = yes }
										var:global.occupied_state = { ALB_is_kosovar_state = yes }
									}
									AND = {
										capital_scope = { ALB_is_northern_state = yes }
										var:global.occupied_state = { ALB_is_northern_state = yes }
									}
									AND = {
										capital_scope = { ALB_is_central_state = yes }
										var:global.occupied_state = { ALB_is_central_state = yes }
									}
									AND = {
										capital_scope = { ALB_is_southern_state = yes }
										var:global.occupied_state = { ALB_is_southern_state = yes }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = ALB
					limit = {
						has_capitulated = no
						has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_idea = ALB_decentralized_independence_movement }
							AND = {
								has_idea = ALB_decentralized_independence_movement
								OR = {
									AND = {
										capital_scope = { ALB_is_kosovar_state = yes }
										OR = {
											var:global.occupied_state = {
												OR = {
													ALB_is_kosovar_state = yes
													has_state_flag = ALB_can_organize_uprisings
													ALB_is_northern_state = yes
												}
											}
											has_country_flag = ALB_can_organize_northern_uprisings
										}
									}
									AND = {
										capital_scope = { ALB_is_northern_state = yes }
										OR = {
											var:global.occupied_state = {
												OR = {
													ALB_is_northern_state = yes
													has_state_flag = ALB_can_organize_uprisings
													ALB_is_kosovar_state = yes
												}
											}
											has_country_flag = ALB_can_organize_northern_uprisings
										}
									}
									AND = {
										capital_scope = { ALB_is_central_state = yes }
										var:global.occupied_state = {
											OR = {
												ALB_is_central_state = yes
												has_state_flag = ALB_can_organize_uprisings
											}
										}
									}
									AND = {
										capital_scope = { ALB_is_southern_state = yes }
										var:global.occupied_state = {
											OR = {
												ALB_is_southern_state = yes
												has_state_flag = ALB_can_organize_uprisings
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
					set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = ALB
					copy_tag = ALB
					transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
					set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
					set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
					set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
					set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
					set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
					set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
					var:global.occupier_country = { remove_from_allowed_party = yes }
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
						var:global.occupied_country = { remove_from_allowed_party = yes }
					}
					set_popularities = { neutrality = 100 }
					set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					if = {
						limit = { capital_scope = { ALB_is_kosovar_state = yes } }
						set_cosmetic_tag = ALB_boletini_flag
						every_other_country = {
							limit = { any_character = { ALB_is_kosovar_character = yes } }

							promote_character = { character = ALB_isa_boletini ideology = warlordism }

						promote_character = { character = ALB_cerciz_topulli ideology = stratocracy }
					}

				limit = { var:global.new_occupied_country = { capital_scope = { ALB_is_northern_state = yes } } }
				hidden_effect = { set_global_flag = ALB_1911_uprising }

			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						original_tag = ALB
						has_idea = ALB_decentralized_independence_movement
					}
					var:global.new_occupied_country = { NOT = { has_idea = ALB_decentralized_independence_movement } }
				}
				var:global.new_occupied_country = {
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ALB_albanian_society_bad }
					set_variable = { ALB_as_political_power_factor = ALB.ALB_as_political_power_factor }
					set_variable = { ALB_as_war_support_factor = ALB.ALB_as_war_support_factor }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = BUL_join_albania_in_the_next_uprising }
				clr_global_flag = BUL_join_albania_in_the_next_uprising
				BUL = { country_event = { id = albania.28 hours = 8 random_days = 2 } }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_core_of = IKR
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = IKR }
			}
			IKR = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				if = {
					limit = { GRE = { has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country } }
					GRE = {
						IKR = { get_current_government_type = yes }
						set_autonomy = {
							target = IKR
							autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_unilateral_union
						}
						IKR = { restore_previous_government_type = yes }
					}
				}
			}

			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {

				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}

			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = { is_core_of = GRE }

					country_exists = GRE

				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = GRE

					set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }

					limit = { state_population > 200000 }

				if = {
					limit = { state_population > 300000 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 1 } 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state_population > 400000 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 1 } 
				}

							end = num_units_to_create

								division = "division_template = \"Kryengritësit Shqiptarë\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 0.4"

						}
					}
					else = {
						for_loop_effect = {
							end = num_units_to_create
							create_unit = {
								division = "division_template = \"Kryengritësit Shqiptarë\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 0.6"
								owner = var:global.new_occupied_country
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = { var:global.occupier_country = { has_completed_focus = TUR_iron_fist_of_the_empire } }

							create_unit = {
								division = "division_template = \"Rebels\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 0.4"
								owner = var:global.new_occupied_country
							}
						}
					}
					else = {
						for_loop_effect = {
							end = num_units_to_create
							create_unit = {
								division = "division_template = \"Rebels\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 0.6"
								owner = var:global.new_occupied_country
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			# create war if necesarry
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_capitulated = yes
						NOT = { has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country }
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = { target = var:global.occupier_country type = annex_everything }
				set_country_flag = TUR_revolting_country
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = MAC
						original_tag = ALB
					}
					has_completed_focus = TUR_elections_of_clubs
					has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country
				}
				var:global.occupier_country = { country_event = { id = ottoman.7 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.new_occupied_country = { original_tag = HJZ }
				var:global.occupier_country = { has_country_flag = TUR_arab_revolt }
			}
			set_global_flag = great_arabian_revolt
			news_event = { id = ww1_hejaz.8 hours = 6 }
		}
		var:global.occupier_country = {
			country_event = ottoman.282
			set_variable = { global.occupied_country_event = global.occupied_country }
			set_variable = { global.occupied_state_event =  global.occupied_state }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Ibrahim Hakki resigns
	id = ottoman.1
	title = ottoman.1.t
	desc = ottoman.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ibrahim_hakki_pasha
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader_with_trait = TUR_unshaken_dignity
		check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var < 50 }
	}
	timeout_days = 14
	option = {
		name = ottoman.1.a
		remove_country_leader_role = {
			character = TUR_ibrahim_hakki
			ideology = authoritarian_democracy
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = TUR_mehmed_said
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				traits = { TUR_kucuk grand_vizier }
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = TUR_government_stability_add_20
			TUR_government_stability_var = 20
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		TUR_government_stability_calculate = yes
		set_country_flag = TUR_mehmed_said_chosen
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.1.b
		remove_country_leader_role = {
			character = TUR_ibrahim_hakki
			ideology = authoritarian_democracy
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = TUR_haci_adil_bey
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				traits = { TUR_peacetime_bureaucrat grand_vizier }
			}
		}
		TUR_haci_adil_bey = { set_character_name = TUR_haci_adil_pasha }
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = TUR_government_stability_add_10
			TUR_government_stability_var = 10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.05

country_event = { #ottomans ask french to join them russia ask ottomans dominion
	id = ottoman.26
	title = ottoman.26.t
	desc = ottoman.26.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.26.a
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = TUR
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_diplomatic_isolation_1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_democratic_party_value
				value = party_popularity@democratic
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_neutrality_party_value
				value = party_popularity@neutrality
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_communism_party_value
				value = party_popularity@communism
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_fascism_party_value
				value = party_popularity@fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = democratic }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_democratic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = communism }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_communist
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_elections = yes }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TUR
				autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				end_wars = yes
				end_civil_wars = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = ottoman_democratic_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = ottoman_neutrality_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = ottoman_communism_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = ottoman_fascism_party_value
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ottomans_are_democratic }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ottomans_are_communist }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
					has_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections }
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ottomans_are_fascism }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.27 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.26.b
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.28 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_state = {

						size > 0

				}

			custom_effect_tooltip = ottoman.48.tt

			set_variable = { dlf_monthly_population = -0.2 }
			force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
		}
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = TUR_starving_syria
		TRS_increase_arab_opposition = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}

		}
		country_event = { id = ottoman.72 days = 180 random_days = 180 }
	}

	title = ottoman.75.t
	desc = ottoman.75.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_sharif_hussein
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.75.a
		679 = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_TUR_arab_minority_tt
			add_to_variable = {
				tooltip = resistance_target_50
				TUR_ottoman_resistance_target_arab = 0.5
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
			add_resistance = 35
			add_compliance = -30
		}
		TUR_minority_revolt_effect = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

country_event = { #ittihadist grand vizier swap
	id = ottoman.77
	title = ottoman.77.t
	desc = ottoman.77.desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_ittihadist_meeting
	option = {
		name = ottoman.77.a
		trigger = { TUR_ibrahim_hakki = { is_country_leader = no } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ibrahim_hakki_remove_first_trait } }
				remove_country_leader_role = {
					character = TUR_ibrahim_hakki
					ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TUR_committee_of_union_and_progress = { is_country_leader = no } }
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_ibrahim_hakki = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy } }
				TUR_ibrahim_hakki = { promote_character = authoritarian_democracy }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = TUR_ibrahim_hakki
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						traits = { TUR_unshaken_dignity grand_vizier }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = { add_stability = 0.05 }
		set_country_flag = TUR_ibrahim_hakki_remove_first_trait
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_empower_the_grand_vizier }
			TUR_add_appropriate_grand_vizier_for_bop = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.77.b
		trigger = { TUR_ali_fuat_turkgeldi = { is_country_leader = no } }
		if = {
			limit = { TUR_committee_of_union_and_progress = { is_country_leader = no } }
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_ali_fuat_turkgeldi = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy } }
				TUR_ali_fuat_turkgeldi = { promote_character = authoritarian_democracy }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = TUR_ali_fuat_turkgeldi
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						traits = { TUR_respectable_oldguard grand_vizier }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_empower_the_grand_vizier }
			TUR_add_appropriate_grand_vizier_for_bop = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.77.c
		trigger = { TUR_said_halim = { is_country_leader = no } }
		if = {
			limit = { TUR_committee_of_union_and_progress = { is_country_leader = no } }
			if = {
				limit = { TUR_said_halim = { has_ideology = authoritarian_democracy } }
				TUR_said_halim = { promote_character = authoritarian_democracy }
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = TUR_said_halim
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democracy
						traits = { TUR_conservative_ittihadist grand_vizier }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = democratic }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = communism }
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_empower_the_grand_vizier }
			TUR_add_appropriate_grand_vizier_for_bop = yes
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.77.d
		trigger = {
			always = no
			TUR_committee_of_union_and_progress = { is_country_leader = no }
			has_completed_focus = TUR_politics_on_connections
		}
		TUR_committee_of_union_and_progress = { promote_character = civilian_dictatorship }
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = TUR_government_stability_reduce_10
			TUR_government_stability_var = -10
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

country_event = { #süleyman askeri suicide
	id = ottoman.78
	title = ottoman.78.t
	desc = ottoman.78.d
	trigger = {
		has_character = TUR_suleyman_askeri
		owns_state = 291
		NOT = { controls_state = 291 }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_suleyman_askeri
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.78.a
		retire_character = TUR_suleyman_askeri
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_utilize_suleyman_askeri }
			activate_decision = TUR_dismiss_suleyman_askeri
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

	id = ottoman.79

	option = {
		name = ottoman.79.a
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 3 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = after_90_days
		effect_tooltip = { add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = -3 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = empty_space
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_purchase_submarines_tt
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = ottoman.80 hours = 8 } } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				add = -15
				FROM = { has_government = fascism }
				OR = {
					tag = ENG
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				FROM = { has_government = democratic }
				OR = {
					tag = ENG
					is_in_faction_with = ENG
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 75
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

			modifier = {

				}
			}
			modifier = {

			modifier = {
				add = 50

country_event = { #frozen foreign assets add
	id = ottoman.108
	title = ottoman.108.t
	desc = ottoman.108.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_duyun_u_umumiye
	option = {
		name = ottoman.108.a
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_after_war = opda_consumer_goods }
				set_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite_after_war = opda_consumer_goods_opposite }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_war
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = FROM.opda_consumer_goods_after_war }
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = FROM.opda_consumer_goods_opposite_after_war }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = opda_consumer_goods
				min = 0
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
				max = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_FROM_war
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = opda_consumer_goods_opposite_after_war }
					add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = opda_consumer_goods_after_war }
					clamp_variable = {
						var = opda_consumer_goods
						max = 0
					}
					clamp_variable = {
						var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
						min = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		TUR_debt_value_check = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = ottoman.108.tt
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

	id = ottoman.114
	title = ottoman.114.t
	desc = ottoman.114.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	trigger = { has_completed_focus = TUR_autonomy_in_administration }
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			25 = { #izmir
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 339
							controls_state = 824
							controls_state = 340
							controls_state = 342
						}
						has_country_flag = TUR_izmir_unionist_autonomy
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.115 days = 70 random_days = 35 }
			}
			25 = { #trabzon
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 354
							controls_state = 355
							controls_state = 1034
						}
						has_country_flag = TUR_trabzon_unionist_autonomy
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.116 days = 70 random_days = 35 }
			}
			25 = { #diyarbakir
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 350
							controls_state = 1028
							controls_state = 884
						}
						has_country_flag = TUR_diyarbakir_unionist_autonomy
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.117 days = 70 random_days = 35 }
			}
			25 = { #edirne
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 756
							controls_state = 341
							controls_state = 860
							controls_state = 200
							controls_state = 849
							controls_state = 757

		}
	}

		name = ottoman.118.a
		TUR = { change_tag_from = ROOT }

			every_character = { set_nationality = TUR }
			TUR = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ROOT
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = TUR_ahmed_cemal }
				TUR_ahmed_cemal = { remove_country_leader_trait = TUR_uncrowned_king }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = TUR_rafiq_al_azm }
				TUR_rafiq_al_azm = { remove_country_leader_role = { ideology = liberal_conservatism } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = TUR_israel_shochat }
				TUR_israel_shochat = { remove_country_leader_role = { ideology = religious_communism } }
			}
			TUR = { country_event = ottoman.119 }
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_idea = TUR_great_famine_of_syria } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_syria_transfer_famine
				meta_effect = {
					text = { set_variable = { global.TUR_gfs_time = [gfs_time] } }
					gfs_time = "[?FROM.TUR_great_famine_of_syria_time:days_left]"
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.119.a
		FROM = { every_character = { set_nationality = TUR } }
		annex_country = {
			target = FROM
			transfer_troops = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_syria_transfer_famine }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_great_famine_of_syria
				days = var:global.TUR_gfs_time
			}
			unlock_decision_category_tooltip = TUR_starving_syria
			clr_country_flag = TUR_syria_transfer_famine
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

			flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_rumelia
			days = 180
			value = 1
		}

			flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_anatolia
			days = 180
			value = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_syria
			days = 180
			value = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_mesapotamia
			days = 180
			value = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = TUR_not_taking_investment_trablusgarp
			days = 180
			value = 1
		}
		add_political_power = 50

						OR = {
							tag = RUS
							is_subject_of = RUS
						}
					}
				}
			}
			855 = { transfer_state_to = TUR }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				420 = {
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = RUS
							is_subject_of = RUS
						}
					}
				}
			}
			420 = { transfer_state_to = PER }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TUR }
			white_peace = RUS
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = RUS }
				ROOT = { white_peace = PREV }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				white_peace = RUS
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_subject_of = RUS }
					PREV.PREV = { white_peace = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = TUR_government_stability_add_20

		TUR_government_stability_calculate = yes
		TUR_government_popularity_calculate = yes

	}

					}
				}
				country_event = ottoman.196
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		all_state = {
			is_core_of = EGY

		}
		surrender_progress > 0.05
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.195.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			white_peace = EGY
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						AND = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							has_autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_ottoman_committee_government
						}
					}
				}
				is_core_of = EGY
			}
			transfer_state_to = EGY
		}
		clr_global_flag = TUR_ottoman_invasion_of_egypt
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

country_event = { #russia forces armenian reforms

	title = ottoman.205.t
	desc = ottoman.205.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #say yes
		name = ottoman.205.a
		TUR = { country_event = { id = ottoman.215 hours = 8 } }
		RUS = { country_event = { id = ottoman.215 hours = 8 } }
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = yenikoy_accord_involved }
			country_event = { id = ottoman.215 hours = 8 }
		}
		event_option_tooltip = ottoman.215.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = GER }
					has_war_with = GER
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = FRA }
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = ENG }
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = ITA }
					has_war_with = ITA
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = RUS
					ratio > 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #involve european powers
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = GER
					NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = FRA
					NOT = { has_war_with = FRA }
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = ENG
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = ITA
					NOT = { has_war_with = ITA }
				}
			}
		}
		name = ottoman.205.b
		country_event = ottoman.206
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = { #say no
		name = ottoman.205.c
		FROM = { country_event = { id = ottoman.211 hours = 8 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = probably_lead_to_war_with_rus_tt
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = RUS
					ratio > 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

					is_subject_of = ROOT

				}
			}
			every_state = {

					}

		}
		else = {
			every_state = {

					owner = { has_country_flag = post_transcaucasia }

						is_core_of = ROOT
						is_claimed_by = ROOT

						state = 855
						state = 787
						state = 806
						state = 816
						state = 939
					}
				}

			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = post_transcaucasia }
				white_peace = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = ARM }
			if = {
				limit = {
					ARA = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						has_autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_ottoman_autonomous_vilayet
					}
				}
				ARA = { annex_country = { target = PREV } }
			}
			else = { give_military_access = ROOT }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				MOU = {
					exists = yes
					is_in_faction = no
					is_subject = no
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
					OR = {
						has_government = ROOT
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
					}
				}
			}
			give_guarantee = MOU
		}
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = ottoman.238 hours = 6 } }
	}
}

							check_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents > 1 }
							has_government = neutrality
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = fascism
						any_country = {
							check_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents > 1 }
							has_government = fascism
						}
					}
					AND = {
						has_government = communism
						any_country = {
							check_variable = { TUR_stolen_documents > 1 }
							has_government = communism
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			remove_decision = TUR_active_submarine_commission

		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = TUR_active_destroyer_commission }
			remove_decision = TUR_active_destroyer_commission

		if = {
			limit = { has_decision = TUR_active_battleship_commission }
			remove_decision = TUR_active_battleship_commission
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = has_active_ship_commission
			clear_variable = var:global.TUR_ship_commission_tag
			if = {
				limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_ship_commission_submarine } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_ship_commission_submarine
			}
			if = {
				limit = { TUR = { has_country_flag = TUR_ship_commission_destroyer } }
				set_country_flag = TUR_ship_commission_destroyer
			}
			if = {

				set_country_flag = TUR_ship_commission_battleship
			}
		}

	}

			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_blocked_famine_reduce_1

			add_to_variable = { global.TUR_gfs_stability_factor = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { global.TUR_gfs_stability_weekly_factor = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { global.TUR_gfs_war_support_weekly_factor = -0.005 }
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_committee_government = yes
					has_state_flag = TUR_syria_famine_state
					check_variable = { TUR_arab_state_level > 0 }
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_blocked_famine_reduce_1_state
				add_to_variable = { dlf_monthly_population = 0.01 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}

country_event = { #ottoman foreign loan
	id = ottoman.260
	title = ottoman.260.t
	desc = ottoman.260.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	option = {
		name = ottoman.260.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
			}
		}
		FRA = { country_event = { id = ottoman.261 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.260.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = GER
				has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
			}
		}
		GER = { country_event = { id = ottoman.261 days = 1 } }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_war_with = FRA
					has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
				}
				add = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.260.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				FRA = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with = GER
				GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
			}
		}
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA_foreign_power }
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
			country_event = { id = ottoman.261 days = 1 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_war_with = FRA
					FRA = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
				}
				OR = {
					has_war_with = GER
					GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
				}
				add = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #ottoman foreign loan with strings
	id = ottoman.263
	title = ottoman.263.t
	desc = ottoman.263.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty3
	option = { #yes
		name = ottoman.263.a
		TUR_add_debt_4_FROM = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_economic_liberalism }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_inflow_of_foreign_loan_3
				days = 1100
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_inflow_of_foreign_loan_2
				days = 1100
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = TUR_foreign_loan_secured
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = ottoman.264 days = 1 } } }
		complete_national_focus = TUR_foreign_loan_negotiations
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FROM = { tag = GER }
						FRA = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = { tag = FRA }
						GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								tag = FRA
								tag = GER
							}
						}
						FRA = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
						GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #no
		name = ottoman.263.b
		trigger = {
			any_other_country = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA_foreign_power }
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
					has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
				country_event = { id = ottoman.265 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = { tag = FRA }
					FRA = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = ottoman.261 days = 1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					FROM = { tag = GER }
					GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
				}
			}
			FRA = { country_event = { id = ottoman.261 days = 1 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_war_with = FRA
					FRA = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
				}
				OR = {
					has_war_with = GER
					GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA_foreign_power }
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
						tag = FROM
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.261 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						FROM = { tag = GER }
						NOT = { FRA = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan } }
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = { tag = FRA }
						NOT = { GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan } }
					}
					AND = {
						FROM = {
							NOT = {
								tag = FRA
								tag = GER
							}
						}
						OR = {
							NOT = { FRA = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan } }
							NOT = { GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan } }
						}
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				OR = {
					has_war_with = GER
					GER = { has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan }
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA_foreign_power }
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
						tag = FROM
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.261 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.266.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_other_country = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA_foreign_power }
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						has_country_flag = TUR_rejected_loan
					}
				}
			}
		}
		TUR_add_debt_1_ALL = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_economic_liberalism }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_inflow_of_foreign_loan_3
				days = 1100
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_inflow_of_foreign_loan_2
				days = 1100
			}
		}
		complete_national_focus = TUR_foreign_loan_negotiations
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

			limit = { has_dlc = "Arms Against Tyranny" }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_equipment_to_add = 1000 }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_equipment_to_multiply = GER.opinion@TUR }
			multiply_temp_variable  = { TUR_equipment_to_multiply = 10 }
			add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_equipment_to_add = TUR_equipment_to_multiply }
			add_equipment_subsidy = {
				cic = var:TUR_equipment_to_add
				equipment_type = tac_bomber_equipment
				seller_tags = { GER }
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_equipment_to_add = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = TUR_a_deal_with_foreign_aircraft_designers }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_equipment_to_multiply = GER.opinion@TUR }
				multiply_temp_variable  = { TUR_equipment_to_multiply = 0.05 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_equipment_to_add = TUR_equipment_to_multiply }
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = tac_bomber_equipment
				amount = var:TUR_equipment_to_add
				producer = GER
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				NOT = { has_equipment = { tac_bomber_equipment > 20 } }
				factor = 100
			}
		}
	}
}

# event for countries under blockade
country_event = {
	id = ottoman.288
	title = ottoman.288.t
	desc = ottoman.288.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_merchant_ship_01
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ottoman.288.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ottoman.288_tt
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = FROM }
				OR = {
					alliance_naval_strength_ratio < 1
					has_idea = GER_famine
					has_idea = GER_food_shortages
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = AUH_famine_effect }
				}
				has_war = yes
				any_owned_state = { is_coastal = yes }
				NOT = { tag = FROM }
			}
			unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_ottoman_backed_blockade_evasion
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ottoman.289
	title = ottoman.289.t
	desc = ottoman.289.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_merchant_ship_01
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ottoman.289.a
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
            type = convoy_1
            amount = -50
        }
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = { add_stability = 0.1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GER_famine }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_famine
					add_idea = GER_food_shortages
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = ottoman.293.t
	desc = ottoman.293.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_gre_balkan_pact
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ottoman.293.a
		add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_balkan_customs_union_dm }
		custom_effect_tooltip = ottoman.293.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { global.BCU_local_resources_factor = 0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { global.BCU_consumer_goods_factor = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { global.BCU_production_factory_max_efficiency_factor = 0.01 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_balkan_customs_union_dm } }
				country_event = { id = ottoman.294 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -30
				}
				add = -10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -60
				}
				add = -10
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.293.b
		hidden_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_balkan_customs_union_dm } }
				country_event = { id = ottoman.295 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 65
				}
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -0
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -25
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -75
				}
				add = 5
			}
		}
	}
}
